Installing MariaDB on Windows 7 64-bit

Hello. I have beeing trying to install MariaDB 64-bit on Windows 7 64-bit. This is a fresh install of Windows 7 with drivers only and few other programs like firewall and web browser. Every time the installation start it comes to the point where mysql_install_db.exe is started and then it rolls back. I have tried to install both MariaDB 10.1.18 Stable 64-bit as well as MariaDB 5.5.53 Stable 64-bit. Amd both installations come out with the same results Rolling back.

What I have also tried is to start the installation with by creating a log file msiexec /i "G:\Install\MariaDB 5.5.53 Stable\mariadb-5.5.53-winx64.msi" /l*v c:\temp\msi_mariadb_5.5.log and I can provied the output of that log file. I have also tried the installation of 32bit MariaDB and it goes thru without any prolbems so I guess there is some kind of bug in the 64-bit installlation package or I am missing some crucial libraries for this install. Any help would be appriciated. Here is the code from the installation logfile

Observe that for the secutiry reasons I have replaced username, computer network name as well as password provided during the installation. What I would like is to get help installing the 64bit of MariaDB on my pc. Or at least a pointer to somewhere where I can get instructions in how to install MariaDB manually.

Thank you Nick

Answer Answered by Vladislav Vaintroub in this comment.

An error report like this (with full MSI log) is better suited for our bug database in JIRA. Bad news for you is that MSI has nothing to do with your problem, it is the server that crashes, as you can find in the log "CAQuietExec: 161025 20:35:45 D:\Program Files\MariaDB 5.5\bin\mysqld.exe (mysqld 5.5.53-MariaDB) starting as process 3424 ... CAQuietExec: 161025 20:35:45 mysqld got exception 0xc000001d ;"

WE had a bug report on that here https://jira.mariadb.org/browse/MDEV-11091, feel free to comment in the issue. I could not reproduce this on any machines I have, nor the original reporter could reproduce it on anything but Xen virtualized box. So it seemed a problem with virtualization to us.
